2025-08-22T17:03:57+0800 iZt4nd3kuaspkb4iyb5vqwZ gunicorn[386187]:   "sql_query": "WITH fy_periods AS (\n  SELECT 'FY23' AS period, '2023-01-30' AS start_date, '2024-01-28' AS end_date\n  UNION ALL\n  SELECT 'FY24' AS period, '2024-01-29' AS start_date, '2025-02-02' AS end_date\n),\ntransactions_with_category AS (\n  SELECT\n    t.customer_code,\n    t.paid_date,\n    t.sku_code,\n    pm.class_name\n  FROM transaction t\n  JOIN product_master pm ON t.sku_code = pm.sku_code\n  WHERE t.customer_code IS NOT NULL\n    AND t.quantity > 0\n    AND t.price IS NOT NULL\n),\nactive_guests_by_period_category AS (\n  SELECT\n    fp.period,\n    twc.class_name,\n    COUNT(DISTINCT twc.customer_code) AS active_guests\n  FROM fy_periods fp\n  JOIN transactions_with_category twc\n    ON twc.paid_date >= fp.start_date AND twc.paid_date <= fp.end_date\n  GROUP BY fp.period, twc.class_name\n),\npositive_transactions_by_period_category AS (\n  SELECT\n    fp.period,\n    twc.class_name,\n    COUNT(*) AS positive_transactions\n  FROM fy_periods fp\n  JOIN transactions_with_category twc\n    ON twc.paid_date >= fp.start_date AND twc.paid_date <= fp.end_date\n  GROUP BY fp.period, twc.class_name\n),\nfrequency_calculation AS (\n  SELECT\n    ag.period,\n    ag.class_name,\n    ag.active_guests,\n    COALESCE(pt.positive_transactions, 0) AS positive_transactions,\n    ROUND(COALESCE(pt.positive_transactions, 0) / ag.active_guests, 2) AS frequency\n  FROM active_guests_by_period_category ag\n  LEFT JOIN positive_transactions_by_period_category pt\n    ON ag.period = pt.period AND ag.class_name = pt.class_name\n)\nSELECT\n  class_name,\n  MAX(CASE WHEN period = 'FY23' THEN frequency END) AS FY23_Frequency,\n  MAX(CASE WHEN period = 'FY24' THEN frequency END) AS FY24_Frequency,\n  ROUND(\n    (MAX(CASE WHEN period = 'FY24' THEN frequency END) - MAX(CASE WHEN period = 'FY23' THEN frequency END))\n    / MAX(CASE WHEN period = 'FY23' THEN frequency END) * 100, 2\n  ) AS YoY_Growth_Rate_Percent\nFROM frequency_calculation\nWHERE class_name IS NOT NULL\nGROUP BY class_name\nHAVING FY23_Frequency IS NOT NULL AND FY24_Frequency IS NOT NULL\nORDER BY YoY_Growth_Rate_Percent DESC;",
